    // UpdateKit Input Conversion 1.1 by Mike Beasley
    const input = ￼;
    const defaultTags = [
      'rc',
      ['beta', 'b'],
      ['alpha', 'a']
    ]

    const name = input['Name'] || input['Shortcut Name'];
    const version = input['Version'] || input['Current Version'];


    const update = input['Update'] ? input['Update'] :
      input['RoutineHub ID'] ? `https://routinehub.co/api/v1/shortcuts/${input['RoutineHub ID']}/versions/latest` :
        input['Update URL'];


    const notes = input['Notes'] ? input['Notes'] :
      input['RoutineHub ID'] ? `https://routinehub.co/shortcut/${input['RoutineHub ID']}/changelog` :
        input['Release Notes URL'];

    const prerelease = input['Prerelease'] || false;
    const inputTags = input['Tags'] ? input['Tags'].reverse() : defaultTags;
    const tags = {};

    const getTagValue = (i) =&gt; (i * -1) - 1;

    inputTags.forEach((tag, i) =&gt; {
      if (typeof (tag) == 'object') {
        tag.forEach((subtag) =&gt; {
          tags[subtag] = getTagValue(i);
        })
      } else {
        tags[tag] = getTagValue(i);
      }
    })

    const output = {
      'Name': name,
      'Version': version,
      'Update': update,
      'Notes': notes,
      'Tags': tags,
      'Prerelease': prerelease
    }
    document.getElementById('output').innerHTML = JSON.stringify(output);

    // UpdateKit Engine 2.0.1 by Mike Beasley

    const shortcutData = ￼;
    const updateInfo = ￼;

    const currentVersion = shortcutData.Version;
    const newVersion = updateInfo.Version;
    const showPrerelease = shortcutData.Prerelease;
    let prerelease = false;
    const tags = shortcutData.Tags;

    const createVersionArray = (version) =&gt; {
      const parts = version.split("-");
      const array = parts[0].split(".");
      if (parts[1]) {
        Object.keys(tags).forEach(tag =&gt; {
          const tagName = parts[1].replace(/[0-9]/g, '');
          if (tagName === tag) {
            prerelease = true;
            const tagVersion = parts[1] &amp;&amp; tagName != parts[1] ? parts[1].match(/\d+/g)[0] : "0";
            array.push(tags[tagName], tagVersion);
          }
        })
      }

      return array;
    }

    const currentArray = createVersionArray(currentVersion);
    const newArray = createVersionArray(newVersion);
    const segments = Math.max(currentArray.length, newArray.length);

    while (currentArray.length &lt; segments) currentArray.push("0");
    while (newArray.length &lt; segments) newArray.push("0");

    console.log(currentArray)
    console.log(newArray)

    let index = 0;
    let updateAvailable = false;

    while (index &lt; segments) {
      const newSegment = parseInt(newArray[index]);
      const currentSegment = parseInt(currentArray[index]);

      console.log(newSegment)
      console.log('vs')
      console.log(currentSegment)
      console.log('break')

      if (currentSegment &gt; newSegment) {
        updateAvailable = false
        index = segments;
      } else if (newSegment &gt; currentSegment) {
        updateAvailable = true
        index = segments;
      }
      index++;
    }

    const canShow = !prerelease || showPrerelease;

    output = {
      "Update Available": updateAvailable &amp;&amp; canShow
    }
    document.getElementById('updateAvailable').innerHTML = JSON.stringify(output);
  &lt;/script&gt;
